## üåü About This Repository

This repository provides a **daily-updated collection** of the latest research papers from arXiv in the following domains:

- üé§ **Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR)**
- üó£Ô∏è **Text-to-Speech (TTS)**
- üåê **Machine Translation**
- ‚ö° **Small Language Models**
- üîÑ **Data Augmentation**
- üé® **Synthetic Generation**

> üìñ Usage instructions: [here](./docs/README.md#usage) | üåê Web version: [GitHub Pages](https://nickdee96.github.io/ASR-TTS-paper-daily/)

> üí° This page is inspired by [cv-arxiv-daily](https://github.com/Vincentqyw/cv-arxiv-daily)

## Small Language Models
